<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1980" title="Grammy Awards of 1980">1980</a> – Best Musical Album for Children, <i>In Harmony: A Sesame Street Record</i> (multiple artist compilation w/ Linda Ronstadt)<sup>1</sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1987" title="Grammy Awards of 1987">1987</a> – Best Country Performance by a Duo or Group with Vocal, <i>Trio</i> (with Dolly Parton and Emmylou Harris)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1988" title="Grammy Awards of 1988">1988</a> – Best Mexican-American Performance, <i>Canciones de Mi Padre</i></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1989" title="Grammy Awards of 1989">1989</a> – Best Pop Vocal Performance by a Duo or Group with Vocal, "Don't Know Much" from <i>Cry Like a Rainstorm, Howl Like the Wind</i> with Aaron Neville</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1990" title="Grammy Awards of 1990">1990</a> – Best Pop Vocal Performance by a Duo or Group with Vocal, "All My Life" from <i>Cry Like a Rainstorm, Howl Like the Wind</i> with Aaron Neville</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1992" title="Grammy Awards of 1992">1992</a> – Best Tropical Latin Album, <i>Frenesi</i></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1993" title="Grammy Awards of 1993">1993</a> – Best Mexican-American Album, <i>Mas Canciones</i></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1996" title="Grammy Awards of 1996">1996</a> – Best Musical Album for Children, <i>Dedicated to the One I Love</i></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1999" title="Grammy Awards of 1999">1999</a> – Best Country Collaboration with Vocals, "After the Gold Rush" from <i>Trio II</i> with Dolly Parton and Emmylou Harris</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_2011" title="Grammy Awards of 2011">2011</a> – Lifetime Achievement Award (Latin Grammy)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_2016" title="Grammy Awards of 2016">2016</a> – Lifetime Achievement Award</li>
</ul>
</div>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1980" title="Grammy Awards of 1980">1980</a> – Best Rock Vocal Performance, Female, "How Do I Make You" from <i>Mad Love</i></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1982" title="Grammy Awards of 1982">1982</a> – Best Pop Vocal Performance, Female, "Get Closer" from the album <i>Get Closer</i></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1982" title="Grammy Awards of 1982">1982</a> – Best Rock Vocal Performance, Female, "Get Closer" from the album <i>Get Closer</i></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1987" title="Grammy Awards of 1987">1987</a> – Best Pop Vocal Performance by a Duo or Group with Vocal, "Somewhere Out There" from the soundtrack to <i>An American Tail</i> with <a href="/wiki/James_Ingram" title="James Ingram">James Ingram</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1989" title="Grammy Awards of 1989">1989</a> – Best Pop Vocal Performance, Female, <i>Cry Like a Rainstorm, Howl Like the Wind</i> with <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Neville" title="Aaron Neville">Aaron Neville</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1999" title="Grammy Awards of 1999">1999</a> – Best Country Album, <i>Trio II</i> with Dolly Parton and Emmylou Harris</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_1999" title="Grammy Awards of 1999">1999</a> – Best Contemporary Folk Album, <i>Western Wall: The Tucson Sessions</i> with Emmylou Harris</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_2002" title="Grammy Awards of 2002">2002</a> – Best Traditional Folk Album, <i><a href="/wiki/Evangeline_Made:_A_Tribute_to_Cajun_Music" title="Evangeline Made: A Tribute to Cajun Music">Evangeline Made: A Tribute to Cajun Music</a></i>, multiple artist compilation, with vocalist <a href="/wiki/Ann_Savoy" title="Ann Savoy">Ann Savoy</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grammy_Awards_of_2006" title="Grammy Awards of 2006">2006</a> – Best Traditional Folk Album, <i>Adieu False Heart</i> with Ann Savoy</li>
</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Discography">Discography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Linda_Ronstadt&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Discography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
